# Climbing

![extrasmall](https://github.com/jottenlips/jottenlips.github.io/blob/main/finding-out-8-30-2025-img/heresy2.jpg?raw=true)

Every February, I climb for charity. This year I will donate $1 for every route or boulder sent to [MICA Project](https://www.mica-project.org/). You can donate to my fundraiser [here](https://ig.me/1SsLF2kgo4a4nXz) or directly on their website.

> Past years:

> [Catalyst Sports 3000ft 2025](https://p2p.onecause.com/challengeforaccess2025/john-franke)

> [Catalyst Sports 3000ft 2024](https://www.mightycause.com/story/Qw3r4g)

> [Paradox Sport Mile 2023](https://paradoxsports.salsalabs.org/paradoxmileclimbnashville2023/p/johnottenlipsfranke/index.html)

> [Paradox Sport Mile 2022](https://www.paradoxsports.org/wp-content/uploads/2022/07/FY22-Annual-Report-FINAL.pdf)

[First time lead climbing outdoors](firsttime/)

[Favorite Spots in the Southeast](southeast/)

[Arizona 2023](arizona-2023/)

[October 2023 Utah](utah-2023/)

[Summer 2025 Obed Project](summer-2025-obed/)

## Indoor Climbing Stats

I have been tracking most of my indoor climbing sessions with a Garmin to get the approximate feet and grade. Sometimes the altimeter is off.
The code to generate these charts can be found here: [Garmin Climbing Charts](https://github.com/jottenlips/garminclimb)

const COLORS = {
  green1: '#2d5016',
  green2: '#3a6b1e',
  green3: '#4a8525',
  leaf: '#6b9e3a',
  sage: '#8fbc6a',
  olive: '#7a8a40',
  tan: '#b5956a',
  brown: '#8a6830',
  sand: '#c4a060',
  rust: '#a06030',
};

const YDS_GRADE_MAP = {
  _5_6:0,_5_7:1,_5_8:2,_5_9:3,
  _5_10A:4,_5_10_MINUS:4,_5_10B:5,_5_10:5,_5_10C:6,_5_10_PLUS:7,_5_10D:7,
  _5_11A:8,_5_11_MINUS:8,_5_11B:9,_5_11:9,_5_11C:10,_5_11_PLUS:11,_5_11D:11,
  _5_12A:12,_5_12_MINUS:12,_5_12B:13,_5_12:13,_5_12C:14,_5_12_PLUS:15,_5_12D:15,
  _5_13A:16,_5_13_MINUS:16,_5_13B:17,_5_13:17,_5_13C:18,_5_13_PLUS:19,_5_13D:19,
  _5_14A:20,_5_14_MINUS:20,_5_14B:21,_5_14:21,_5_14C:22,_5_14_PLUS:23,_5_14D:23,
};

const GRADE_LABELS = ['5.6','5.7','5.8','5.9','5.10a','5.10b','5.10c','5.10d',
  '5.11a','5.11b','5.11c','5.11d','5.12a','5.12b','5.12c','5.12d',
  '5.13a','5.13b','5.13c','5.13d','5.14a','5.14b','5.14c','5.14d'];

function numberToGrade(n) { return GRADE_LABELS[n] || `${n}`; }
function metersToFeet(m) { return Math.round(m * 3.28084); }

function getActiveSplit(activity) {
  const s = activity?.splitSummaries;
  if (!s || !s.length) return null;
  return s[0]?.splitType === 'CLIMB_ACTIVE' ? {...s[0], start: activity.startTimeLocal} : {...s[1], start: activity.startTimeLocal};
}

function chartDefaults() {
  Chart.defaults.color = '#555';
  Chart.defaults.borderColor = '#e0e0d8';
  Chart.defaults.font.family = "-apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif";
  Chart.defaults.font.size = 11;
}

function makeCanvas(parentId) {
  const box = document.createElement('div');
  box.className = 'chart-box';
  const canvas = document.createElement('canvas');
  box.appendChild(canvas);
  document.getElementById(parentId).appendChild(box);
  return canvas.getContext('2d');
}

function barChart(ctx, labels, data, title, color, yCallback) {
  new Chart(ctx, {
    type: 'bar',
    data: {
      labels,
      datasets: [{
        label: title,
        data,
        backgroundColor: color + 'bb',
        borderColor: color,
        borderWidth: 1,
        borderRadius: 3,
      }]
    },
    options: {
      responsive: true,
      maintainAspectRatio: true,
      plugins: {
        legend: { display: false },
        title: { display: true, text: title, color: '#2d5016', font: { size: 13, weight: '600' } }
      },
      scales: {
        y: { beginAtZero: true, ticks: { callback: yCallback || (v => v), font: { size: 10 } }, grid: { color: '#e8e8e0' } },
        x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { font: { size: 10 }, maxRotation: 45 } }
      }
    }
  });
}

function lineChart(ctx, labels, data, title, color, yCallback, integerOnly) {
  new Chart(ctx, {
    type: 'line',
    data: {
      labels,
      datasets: [{
        label: title,
        data,
        borderColor: color,
        backgroundColor: color + '22',
        fill: true,
        tension: 0.3,
        pointRadius: 3,
        pointBackgroundColor: color,
        borderWidth: 2,
      }]
    },
    options: {
      responsive: true,
      maintainAspectRatio: true,
      plugins: {
        legend: { display: false },
        title: { display: true, text: title, color: '#2d5016', font: { size: 13, weight: '600' } }
      },
      scales: {
        y: { beginAtZero: false, ticks: { callback: yCallback || (v => v), font: { size: 10 }, stepSize: integerOnly ? 1 : undefined }, grid: { color: '#e8e8e0' } },
        x: { grid: { display: false }, ticks: { font: { size: 10 }, maxRotation: 45 } }
      }
    }
  });
}

function processAndRender(indoorData, boulderData) {
  chartDefaults();

  const indoorSplits = indoorData.map(getActiveSplit).filter(Boolean);
  const boulderSplits = boulderData.map(getActiveSplit).filter(Boolean).filter(s => s.noOfSplits !== 1);

  function groupByMonthYear(splits, valueFn) {
    const map = {};
    splits.forEach(s => {
      const [date] = s.start.split(' ');
      const [y, m] = date.split('-');
      const key = `${y}-${m}`;
      map[key] = valueFn(s, map[key]);
    });
    return map;
  }

  function aggregateByYear(monthly, mode) {
    const map = {};
    Object.entries(monthly).forEach(([key, val]) => {
      const year = key.split('-')[0];
      if (mode === 'max') map[year] = Math.max(map[year] || 0, val);
      else map[year] = (map[year] || 0) + val;
    });
    const sorted = Object.entries(map).sort((a, b) => parseInt(b[0]) - parseInt(a[0]));
    return { labels: sorted.map(e => e[0]), values: sorted.map(e => e[1]) };
  }

  const feetByMonth = groupByMonthYear(indoorSplits, (s, prev) => (prev || 0) + metersToFeet(s.totalAscent));
  const boulderFeetByMonth = groupByMonthYear(boulderSplits, (s, prev) => (prev || 0) + s.noOfSplits * 10);
  const combinedFeetByMonth = {};
  Object.keys(feetByMonth).forEach(k => combinedFeetByMonth[k] = feetByMonth[k] + (boulderFeetByMonth[k] || 0));
  const maxGradeByMonth = groupByMonthYear(indoorSplits, (s, prev) => Math.max(prev || 0, YDS_GRADE_MAP[s.maxGradeValue?.valueKey] || 0));
  const maxBoulderGradeByMonth = groupByMonthYear(boulderSplits, (s, prev) => Math.max(prev || 0, parseInt(s.maxGradeValue?.valueKey?.replace(/\D/g, '')) || 0));
  const ropeSessionsByMonth = groupByMonthYear(indoorSplits, (s, prev) => (prev || 0) + 1);
  const boulderSessionsByMonth = groupByMonthYear(boulderSplits, (s, prev) => (prev || 0) + 1);

  // Stats summary
  const totalFeet = Object.values(combinedFeetByMonth).reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0);
  const totalRoutes = indoorSplits.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.numClimbSends || 0), 0);
  const totalFalls = indoorSplits.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.numFalls || 0), 0);
  const totalBoulders = boulderSplits.reduce((a, s) => a + (s.noOfSplits || 0), 0);
  const avgMaxGrade = Math.round(indoorSplits.reduce((a, s) => a + (YDS_GRADE_MAP[s.maxGradeValue?.valueKey] || 0), 0) / indoorSplits.length);
  const bestGrade = Math.max(...indoorSplits.map(s => YDS_GRADE_MAP[s.maxGradeValue?.valueKey] || 0));
  const bestBoulderGrade = Math.max(...boulderSplits.map(s => parseInt(s.maxGradeValue?.valueKey?.replace(/\D/g, '')) || 0));

  document.getElementById('stats-summary').innerHTML = [
    ['Total Feet', `${totalFeet.toLocaleString()} ft`],
    ['Routes Sent', totalRoutes],
    ['Falls', totalFalls],
    ['Boulders', totalBoulders],
    ['Avg Max Grade', numberToGrade(avgMaxGrade)],
    ['Best Rope', numberToGrade(bestGrade)],
    ['Best Boulder', `V${bestBoulderGrade}`],
  ].map(([l, v]) => `<div class="stat-card"><div class="label">${l}</div><div class="value">${v}</div></div>`).join('');

  // Yearly
  const yearlyBar = [
    [combinedFeetByMonth, 'sum', 'Total Feet By Year (Combined)', COLORS.green1],
    [feetByMonth, 'sum', 'Route Feet By Year', COLORS.green3],
    [boulderFeetByMonth, 'sum', 'Boulder Feet By Year', COLORS.olive],
    [ropeSessionsByMonth, 'sum', 'Rope Sessions By Year', COLORS.tan],
    [boulderSessionsByMonth, 'sum', 'Boulder Sessions By Year', COLORS.brown],
  ];
  yearlyBar.forEach(([monthly, mode, title, color]) => {
    const { labels, values } = aggregateByYear(monthly, mode);
    barChart(makeCanvas('yearly-charts'), labels, values, title, color);
  });
  const yrGrade = aggregateByYear(maxGradeByMonth, 'max');
  lineChart(makeCanvas('yearly-charts'), yrGrade.labels, yrGrade.values, 'Max Rope Grade By Year', COLORS.leaf, v => numberToGrade(v));
  const yrBoulder = aggregateByYear(maxBoulderGradeByMonth, 'max');
  lineChart(makeCanvas('yearly-charts'), yrBoulder.labels, yrBoulder.values, 'Max Boulder Grade By Year', COLORS.rust, v => `V${v}`, true);

  // Monthly
  function monthlyEntries(map) {
    return Object.entries(map).sort((a, b) => b[0].localeCompare(a[0]));
  }
  [
    [combinedFeetByMonth, 'Total Feet By Month (Combined)', COLORS.green1, 'bar'],
    [feetByMonth, 'Route Feet By Month', COLORS.green3, 'bar'],
    [boulderFeetByMonth, 'Boulder Feet By Month', COLORS.olive, 'bar'],
    [maxGradeByMonth, 'Max Rope Grade By Month', COLORS.leaf, 'line', v => numberToGrade(v)],
    [maxBoulderGradeByMonth, 'Max Boulder Grade By Month', COLORS.rust, 'line', v => `V${v}`, true],
    [ropeSessionsByMonth, 'Rope Sessions By Month', COLORS.tan, 'bar'],
    [boulderSessionsByMonth, 'Boulder Sessions By Month', COLORS.brown, 'bar'],
  ].forEach(([map, title, color, type, yCb, intOnly]) => {
    const entries = monthlyEntries(map);
    const ctx = makeCanvas('monthly-charts');
    if (type === 'line') lineChart(ctx, entries.map(e => e[0]), entries.map(e => e[1]), title, color, yCb, intOnly);
    else barChart(ctx, entries.map(e => e[0]), entries.map(e => e[1]), title, color, yCb);
  });

  // Per-session rope
  const ropeLabels = indoorSplits.map(s => s.start.split(' ')[0]);
  [
    [indoorSplits.map(s => YDS_GRADE_MAP[s.maxGradeValue?.valueKey] || 0), 'Max Grade Per Session', COLORS.green2, 'line', v => numberToGrade(v)],
    [indoorSplits.map(s => s.numClimbSends || 0), 'Sends Per Session', COLORS.tan, 'bar'],
    [indoorSplits.map(s => metersToFeet(s.totalAscent || 0)), 'Feet Per Session', COLORS.green3, 'bar'],
    [indoorSplits.map(s => Math.round((s.duration || 0) / 60)), 'Active Minutes Per Session', COLORS.olive, 'bar'],
  ].forEach(([data, title, color, type, yCb]) => {
    const ctx = makeCanvas('session-rope-charts');
    if (type === 'line') lineChart(ctx, ropeLabels, data, title, color, yCb);
    else barChart(ctx, ropeLabels, data, title, color, yCb);
  });

  // Per-session boulder
  const boulderLabels = boulderSplits.map(s => s.start.split(' ')[0]);
  [
    [boulderSplits.map(s => parseInt(s.maxGradeValue?.valueKey?.replace(/\D/g, '')) || 0), 'Max Boulder Grade Per Session', COLORS.rust, 'line', v => `V${v}`, true],
    [boulderSplits.map(s => s.noOfSplits || 0), 'Splits Per Session', COLORS.brown, 'bar'],
    [boulderSplits.map(s => Math.round((s.duration || 0) / 60)), 'Active Minutes Per Session', COLORS.leaf, 'bar'],
  ].forEach(([data, title, color, type, yCb, intOnly]) => {
    const ctx = makeCanvas('session-boulder-charts');
    if (type === 'line') lineChart(ctx, boulderLabels, data, title, color, yCb, intOnly);
    else barChart(ctx, boulderLabels, data, title, color, yCb);
  });

  document.getElementById('load-prompt').style.display = 'none';
}

// Data loading
async function tryLoadFromPath() {
  try {
    const [a, b] = await Promise.all([fetch('indoor_climbing.json'), fetch('bouldering.json')]);
    if (a.ok && b.ok) { processAndRender(await a.json(), await b.json()); return true; }
  } catch(e) {}
  return false;
}

document.getElementById('fileInput').addEventListener('change', async (e) => {
  const files = Array.from(e.target.files);
  const indoor = files.find(f => f.name.toLowerCase().includes('indoor'));
  const boulder = files.find(f => f.name.toLowerCase().includes('boulder'));
  if (indoor && boulder) {
    processAndRender(await indoor.text().then(JSON.parse), await boulder.text().then(JSON.parse));
  } else {
    alert('Please select both indoorClimbingActivities.json and boulderingActivities.json');
  }
});

(async () => {
  if (typeof INDOOR_DATA !== 'undefined' && typeof BOULDER_DATA !== 'undefined') {
    processAndRender(INDOOR_DATA, BOULDER_DATA);
  } else if (!(await tryLoadFromPath())) {
    document.getElementById('load-prompt').style.display = 'block';
  }
})();
</script>
</body>
</html>
